## High-Level Map

### Pages Overview

- **browser_new_tab**: Microsoft Edge New Tab
  - Browser new tab page with search/address bar focused and a query for the target Viva Learning course already entered.
- **bing_search_results**: Bing search results for Security Foundations: Secure on the Go Viva Learning
  - Search engine results page listing results related to Viva Learning and security topics. The exact target course page is not yet visible in the current viewport.
- **bing_search_results_mid**: Bing search results for Security Foundations: Secure on the Go Viva Learning
  - Mid-page Bing results showing generic Viva Learning support and blog links plus an image strip related to security foundations. The exact course page is still not visible.
- **course_security_foundations_secure_on_the_go**: Security Foundations: Secure on the Go
  - Viva Learning course page for the target course. Header and breadcrumb are visible; main course content area is currently blank/loading in the viewport.

  - The course video page is overlaid by a troubleshooting modal suggesting viewing the course content in the browser if playback issues occur.
- **viva_learning_home**: Home | Viva Learning
  - Main Viva Learning landing page with top navigation, search, personalized welcome panel, featured/trending courses, suggested skills, and recommended learning cards.
- **my_learning_assigned_to_you**: Assigned to you | Viva Learning
  - My Learning page focused on assigned courses. The current tab shows no outstanding assignments and offers a Browse courses button, with additional tabs for bookmarked, collections, recommended, in progress, completed, and LinkedIn Learning content.
- **my_learning_bookmarked**: Bookmarked | Viva Learning
  - My Learning bookmarked tab showing one saved course card on the left and a large empty-state panel encouraging users to save interesting items for later.
- **my_learning_collections**: Collections | Viva Learning
  - My Learning collections tab showing no existing collections and prompting the user to create a new collection to group and share content with peers.
- **my_learning_recommended**: Recommended to you | Viva Learning
  - My Learning recommendations tab showing no received recommendations yet, with a prompt to recommend a course to someone else and a Browse courses button.
- **my_learning_in_progress**: In progress | Viva Learning
  - My Learning tab listing courses currently in progress. Three course cards are visible, including the target course, alongside a placeholder panel for recently opened courses.
- **course_security_foundations_secure_on_the_go_playback_loading**: Security Foundations: Secure on the Go | Playback Loading

### General Patterns

- Browser new tab page with central search box and shortcut tiles.
- Search suggestions appear while typing in the search box.
- Standard Bing results layout with category tabs and organic results.
- Need to scan results for exact course title or Viva Learning app link.
- Search results include generic support/blog content and image strips before any exact course result.
- Direct URL navigation is likely more efficient than continuing search result scanning.
- Viva Learning uses a persistent top navigation bar and breadcrumb trail on course pages.
- Course content may load asynchronously inside a dark themed content panel.
- Course page centers a large video player above additional content.
- Persistent top navigation and breadcrumb remain visible while viewing course content.
- Utility icons appear both in the header and as a small bottom-right overlay.
- Course page is primarily a single-video experience with header actions and footer legal/share links.
- Metadata/details may be hidden behind header utility icons rather than shown inline.
- Troubleshooting modal can appear over the video player without leaving the course page.
- Modal provides a single dismiss action and references viewing content in browser.
- Footer legal/share links remain visible even when modal is open.
- This course appears to be a single embedded video experience rather than a multi-step lesson page.
- Header breadcrumb provides the main route back to the broader Viva Learning app.
- Footer legal/share links persist across the course page.
- The course player is a mostly self-contained single-page video experience.
- Breadcrumb/logo may not navigate when embedded in this frame; Close is the clearest exit path.
- Header utilities and footer legal links persist on the player page.
- Top-level navigation persists across Viva Learning pages: Home, My Learning, Academies, Manage.
- Home page combines personalized summary, featured/trending courses, skill personalization, and recommended course carousels.
- Course cards consistently show title plus metadata like type and duration or rating/learner counts.
- My Learning uses a persistent hero with search plus a horizontal set of content-status tabs with item counts.
- Empty tabs show a centered illustration, explanatory text, and a CTA button.
- Top-level Viva Learning navigation remains consistent with Home, My Learning, Academies, and Manage.
- My Learning sub-tabs persist across all subpages with counts in parentheses.
- Non-empty tabs can still include a large helper/empty-state style panel alongside content cards.
- Course cards consistently include thumbnail, duration badge, title, type, rating/learner count, and overflow menu.
- Empty My Learning tabs use a centered illustration, short explanatory text, and a primary CTA button.
- The same hero banner and sub-tab strip persist across My Learning subpages.
- Collections introduces a creation workflow rather than course cards when empty.
- Several My Learning tabs are empty-state pages with a single centered panel and CTA.
- Sub-tab counts indicate where richer content is likely available; In progress and Completed are the most content-heavy next targets.
- Top-level and sub-level navigation remain consistent across My Learning pages.
- Content-bearing My Learning tabs display course cards in a grid, each with thumbnail, duration badge, title, type, rating/learner count, and overflow menu.
- A helper panel can occupy the right side even when the tab contains course cards.

**Page-Level Patterns:**

- This learning path page uses expandable curriculum sections with module cards instead of a related-courses carousel.
- Header shows aggregate metadata such as item count and total duration.
- Each module card includes its own metadata row plus bookmark/share/more-actions controls and a status indicator.
- Each curriculum section in this learning path currently contains exactly one item and a dedicated Mark complete button.
- Optional sections are labeled explicitly and can include either modules or full learning paths.
- Section descriptions may be truncated with a Read More link.
- Later sections in the learning path include non-course resources such as user-generated web links/documents.
- Each section still provides a Mark complete button even for URL/document resources.
- Some path items can be unavailable and display an inactive/deleted error instead of a normal card.
- The learning path continues with many one-item sections, each pairing a section description with a single Microsoft Learn module card.
- Unavailable items remain listed as sections with duration and title but no clickable card.
- Generative AI-related sections follow the same repeated pattern: section header, description, card, ellipsis, and Mark complete button.
